(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

    (at ?l - location)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)

    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

You have already generated df and pf files according to the observations.
This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (connected ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (closed ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
    (open ?l1 - location ?l2 - location ?d - direction)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)) (open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)
